10a6(rgyud): can gyis lha rnams li/ gus par gsil ba btab par bya// gang gi dkyil 'khor yin pa'i sngags// de la thog maru gsol btag// go rims de'i tshul gyis ni// lha rnams kun gyis btab /

10a8(rgyud): dkyil 'khor bri bar bya// bcom ldan bdag ni gse po la// de bras gnang bar mdzad pa rigs// sangs rgyas 'jig rten mgon rtse dang // bang chub sems dpa' dag bcom 'dang // gsang sngags lnga
10b1(rgyud): gzhan gang lags dang // 'jig rten skyong ba'i lha rnams dang // gang yang 'byung po mthu chen dang // gang su rdo rje lha'i saspyan mnga' ba'i// sems can rnams la snyan la mngon dga' rnams// bdag la dgod
10b2(rgyud): par mdzad du gsol// bdag ming 'di zhes bgyi ba yis// sa 'dir dkyil 'khor bzang po'i ming // 'di zhes bya ba ci nus kyis// cho ga bzhin du bris lags na// bdag dang slob mar bcas pa la// 
10b3(rgyud): thugs ni rtse bar dgongs na su/ tshogs pa thams cad dkyil 'khor du// byin gyis rlob par mdzad du gsol// de ltar lan gsum smras nas ni// bsam pa dag pas phyag byas te// stong pa'i

10b6(rgyud): rdzimamo sangs rgyas mthong na ni// yon tan rgya mtsho mngon sum zhing / mchod rten dang ni sku gzugs mthong // de ma mchod pa brtson pa dang // dge slong dag la chos nyan nam// yang na gnan
10b7(rgyud): la nyan yang rung // chos ni rnam por spyod pa dang // de bzhin glegs bam klog pa dang // rmi lam dge 'dun mthong ba dang // yang na dge slong gcig pu mthong // de dag 'grogs shing rnam zer dang
10b8(rgyud): yang na dge slong dngos por 'gyur// gtsug lag khang dag mthong ba dang / nade bzhin dge slong ma dag n+ya thong / rgyal bya'i sras dag mthong ba dang // de bzhin pa ma bla ma dang // mdza'o nam
11a1(rgyud): rnam pa sna tshogs rnams// rmi lam na ni mthong ba shis/ kaurig sngags dang ni dngos grub thob// de bzhin slob ma 'dzin pa dang // kun dga' rnam pa sna tshogasamathong //

11a3(rgyud): ze dang // byug po skyes bu dam pa dang / ba dang rta dang ngang pa dang // seng ge dang ni ri dgas dang // rmi lam du ni mthong na shes// bkra shis pa'i bya rnams dang // gser bdag gi ni gtu

11a5(rgyud): tog dang // rgyan ni rnam pa tshogs dang // kha bzas dang ni brgyan rnams dang // byis pa dang ni gzhon nu dang // bu med gzugs ni bzang mo dang // rmi lam du ni mthong na
11a6(rgyud): bzang // yang na thob cing rigs sgra dang // rmi lam du ni dbang bskur dang // rgyal por 'gyur ba'i sbyor ba dang // dmig dpon du ni 'gyur ba dang // g.yul las rgyal dang dgra gsod dang /

11a8(rgyud): du ni mthing na dge/ yam shing me la sbyin byed // bya ba bzang po dag la 'jug/ tshwa las rgal dang ro las nal// rkun po dang ni tshar gcod dang stobs 'gyed pa dag rgyal ba dang // gya stobs
11b1(rgyud): rdob cing rgod pa dang // rtse mo sna tshogs rmi ba dang // de bzhin rtsal gzungs byed pa dang // bkra shis dag ni thams cad kyang // mthong bar rab tu dge bar bshad// gsang sngags chos gnyan pa dang
11b2(rgyud): dga' sngon dge ba mthong ba dang // sgrub pa bzang po brtson dang // de la sogs po'i bltas rnams ni// dge ba rnam pa du ma dag/ blo yis rnam par sbyang bya zhing // de las zlog pa spang bar bya// dge ba rnams ni
11b3(rgyud): grub par 'gyur// mi dge rnams ni mi 'grub go/ mi dge ba dag shes nas su// de dag mkhas pas spang bar bya// dge ba yi ni las rnams ni// rab dang 'bring dang tha dad // gsang sngags dngos grub
11b4(rgyud): nas gsum ga/ rab dang 'bring dang tha ma grub// mi dgatsA pA la bzhi pa yi// sbyin sreg zhi ba'i gsang sngags kyis// bla'i mar la brgya rtsa brgyad// cho ga bzhin du zhi bar bar bya//

11b8(rgyud): sngo dang ljang nag po ste/ mtshon rtsi rnams kyang de dang 'dra// dkon mAn+yo g+ha gsum la mchod pa zhing / lha rnams la yang phyag byas nas// mkhas pas srad bu bri bar ba// nang par nyi ma shwa ro ba'i rtse/ 
12a1(rgyud): sa phyogs rgya lcag lo// dengo mos mnyam ste bzung // slob dpon byang du kha lngas te// de nas g.yas phyogs bskor nas ni// bdag nyid nub phyogs kha nga

12a8(rgyud): bro sgo bzhir bya// nub phyogs sgo'am yang na ni// gang lani dza snyid ba gad pa bzhin// de dag rnams ni thams cad kyi// rnam par dbye ba yin par grags// lha mo'i gtso bor gyur pa rnas
12b1(rgyud): rtag tu dkyil 'khor bkod par bya/ de'i lhag ma'i dkyil 'khor ni// gnyis pa dag tu dgod par bya// 'jig rten skyong ba la sogs pa// dkyil 'khor gsum par bsdu bar bya// de las gzhan nas

12b3(rgyud): shin tu ran be dag kya dri zhim re gra na bde ba dang // legs par bkral dang 'phra ba dang // sbom 'phra la sogs bkal legs dang // mdzur mdud med par gyur pa yi// thig skud me tog spos mchod pas/

12b6(rgyud): bros me ga se byer thugro bo ti ga dru khyim po'i dpyad la ci 'byung ba'o// sa'i nges pa de dang 'dra// de nas bla ma'i ci 'byor pa'i// 'phags pa dge 'dun chos ston gsol// yang na bla mas skos pa yi//

13a1(rgyud): byams pa'i sems ni nyer gzhag nas// dkyil 'khon gyi ni drong dro 'ongs// bla ma tshogs rnams kun bsregs shing / lnga ba ngan pa thams cad spangs// dkyil 'khor bri bra tha la/

13a3(rgyud): bradab cing phyag bdaro bya ni yid bzhin mos par bya ba'i phyir// metog sil ma gto re bar bya// srad bu dag gis yongasu bskorargyal mtshan rje babros dag gis brgyan// rgyus pa'i phreng bas

14a1(rgyud): dkar la sogs pa// dad cing yon tan ldan pa 'i// slob mas rin chen bye mas bris// rimatshon lcags rnams me 'byor na/ selu btags pa'i bye mas gya// mchen rtsi lnga

36a1(rgyud): brgyad kyi bye ma snyed kyis gsungs pa/ byin gyis brlabs dang / su yi rang bar mdzad pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi phyag rgyas btab skye/ sems can thams

273b1(rgyud): de nas dpal nag po chen pos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das dam tshig cho ga ji ltar lags// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ bla ma sangs rgyas thaMd dang // dpal ldan nag po chen po yi// rtag tu yid
273b2(rgyud): la gnas par bya// dpal ldan nag po chen po yaM// sngags dang phyag rgya bsam rtan la// yid kyis som nyi med par bya// yongs su ma smin sen dang // bla ma rdo rje 'dzin spong ba// dam tshig bral bar byed pa dang // 
273b3(rgyud): rgyal ba'i bstan pa 'jig byed pa// dpal ldan po chen po yi// dbasam rtan sngags ldan ldan gyur nas// snying rjes bral bar ma byas na// rnal 'byor nges par bshad par bya// dpal ldan nag po sgrub pa
273b4(rgyud): des// sku dang gri gug thod pa dang // 'thun pa'i dam rdzas la sogs pa// de dag rtag tu sba bar bya// brgyud dang sngags kyi don rnams dang // nag po'i bsam rten cho gar byas// kun la/ 
273b5(rgyud): bstan par mi bya ste// btud rtsi lnga dang sreg rdzas dang ka sha chen nya sha chad dang ni// dag gi la du la sogs pa// 'thun par dam rdzas thams cad ni// rtag tu rnal 'byor pa yis sten// dpal ldan na
273b6(rgyud): po chen po yaM// sku dang gri gug thod pa dang // ne reng su la sogs pa yi// bla mas rab tu gnas byas te// dus gsum 'thun pa'i rdzas kyis mchod// rtag tu tshogs kyi 'khor lo yis// dpal ldan nag
273b7(rgyud): sgrub 'dod pas// bla mas rjes su gnang par byed// des ni dpal ldan blo sgrub// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// bstan pa gnas par byed pa ni// dam tshig chen po rab tu ba shA da/ kun la stan
273b8(rgyud): par mi bya ste// gal te rmongs par stan gyur na// ardza ka'i 'bras bu lta re// mgo bo lus po 'gas 'gyur te// dmyal bar nges par ltung bar 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/
